</div></div></div><div class="grid-x grid-margin-x grid-margin-y"><div class="cell small-6"><likes-rating :perfume_id="30947" chart="show" type-chart="small-chart" colors="retro"></likes-rating></div><div class="cell small-6"><seasons-rating :perfume_id="30947" chart="show" type-chart="small-chart" colors="retro"></seasons-rating></div><div class="small-12 medium-6 text-center" style="max-height: 50px"><div itemprop="aggregateRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/AggregateRating" itemscope><p class="info-note">Perfume rating&nbsp;<span itemprop="ratingValue">4.45</span>&nbsp;out of&nbsp;<span itemprop="bestRating">5</span> with&nbsp;<span itemprop="ratingCount" content="13316">13,316</span> votes<meta itemprop="reviewCount" content="1572"/></p></div></div></div><div class="grid-x grid-margin-x grid-margin-y"><div class="cell small-12" itemprop="description" v-pre><p><b>Ultra Male</b> by <b>Jean Paul Gaultier</b> is a Oriental Fougere fragrance for men. <b>Ultra Male</b> was launched in 2015. The nose behind this fragrance is Francis Kurkdjian. Top notes are Pear, Lavender, Mint, Bergamot and Lemon; middle notes are Cinnamon, Clary Sage and Caraway; base notes are Black Vanilla Husk, Amber, Patchouli and Cedar. </p><div v-pre class='fragrantica-blockquote'><p>Jean Paul Gaultier launches its new fragrance Ultra Male in summer 2015. The fragrance is a reinterpretation or enhanced version of the popular original Le Male from 1995. Ultra Male, announced as masculine, intense, seductive and at the same time delicate, is supposedly built on contrasts notes and is a spicier version of the original.
</p>

<p>
It opens with citrus notes of bergamot, along with juicy pear, black lavender and mint. The heart includes spices of cumin and cinnamon, with aromatic clary sage. The base consists of black vanilla, amber and woods. It is signed by Francis Kurkdjian.
 </p>

<p>
The face of the advertising campaign is model Jarrod Scott. The fragrance arrives in a characteristic torso bottle, this time colored in dark blue with black stripes. It is available as 40, 75 and 125 ml Eau de Toilette Intense.</p></div><p class="reviewstrigger" style="font-size: smaller; color: #83a6c4">Read about this perfume in other languages: <a This fragrance has an EXTREME DIFFERENCE BETWEEN WET AND DRY. <br />
Kinda like Malt by Mugler when difference between wet and dry are immense. <br />
Don't forget you're paying for the hours of dry down not the few seconds of juice. <br />
It's not dated stinky, but spice without sweetness, the pink bubble gum will fade. :(<br />
Since the dry down is what matters TEST BEFORE BUYING. Could be pricy considering how much you have to spray. <br />
You'll have to spray a lot of it on fabric (clothes) to get noticed. <br />
Unlike most, I do think it's an office scent. It's pleasantly blended and non offensive. <br />
It gets hate due to homophobia not because anything related to the smell (some men can't stand pink bubblegum notes on a black males perfume) <br />
NOT - A - BLIND - BUY. <br />
Although all TikTok and YouTube Jeremy's this will not be a compliment beast. <br />

Until i smelt this i had this image in my head of a synthetic, young, sweet and boring fragrance. This is not what Ultra Male is. I mostly smell this fruity sweet pear, the pear isnt really fresh but more of a candied pear. With some spice in the background, its not a strong spice, its this mellow and cozy spice. And vanilla as the backbone that you can pick up throughout the journey of the fragrance. It is a little linear but not in a bad way. Its not overly sweet. The scent definitely leans younger, under 30 id say. To my nose this is excellent perfumery and smells gorgeous, great longevity and projection, my fav Jpg and a strong 8/10😼</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="30947"comment_id="2281927"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Jean-Paul-Gaultier/Ultra-Male-30947.html?ccid=2281927#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2279280" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.89);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2279280" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Vilim20014"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1545396"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/himg/o.69247.png" class="comments-avatar"alt="Vilim20014" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2279280ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck0x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2279280" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.89); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1545396">Vilim20014</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-09-11">09/11/24 11:26</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Fruity vanilla with a hint of aromatic and spicy notes. The first thing that jumps out is the sweetness. And it's strong. And fruity. And you absolutely get a lot of vanilla throughout. The second thing you will notice is a hint of green, aromatic notes (mint, lavender, citrus) which is kind of in the background playing a supporting role, as well as a sort of "savory" spiciness, which is reminiscent of caraway, but it's not too strong. I don't get a lot of cinnamon from this.<br />
<br />
Overall a pretty great fragrance if you like sweetness. It definitely smells similar to the original Le Male, but it's much sweeter and denser. I consider this a bit of a negative since it smells kinda dated in my opinion. It doesn't smell anything like Le Parfum or Elixir, which are both far more modern in comparison. And I guess I would have preferred a little bit less freshness from this. I get strong fall vibes from this, which is awesome.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="30947"comment_id="2279280"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Jean-Paul-Gaultier/Ultra-Male-30947.html?ccid=2279280#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2278539" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.76);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2262501" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="SmellSharpe"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1447620"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1447620.gif" class="comments-avatar"alt="SmellSharpe" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Viktor-Rolf/Spicebomb-13857.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.13857.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Spicebomb"title="Spicebomb"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2262501ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck0x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2262501" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.79); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1447620">SmellSharpe</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-08-27">08/27/24 08:00</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Review based on a 03/2024 75ml bottle.<br />
<br />
This is a sweet vanilla, cinnamon, lavender and amber cool weather fragrance. There is a bit of mint, wood and citrus, but this dries down to sweet woody vanilla.<br />
<br />
Definitely masculine and is ideal for a younger crowd. I am not a clubbing guy, but this would be the perfect fragrance for clubs. Absolutely not something I would recommend wearing to the beach. 🤪<br />
<br />
This is an EDT “Intense” but lasts like an EDP. It is strong, in your face and long lasting.<br />
<br />
Excellent fragrance that is true to the JPG DNA.<br />
<br />
Not sure if it is discontinued or has limited regional distribution, but my bottle was produced this year (#408011 - March 2024).</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2071768">dudegetsmoney</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-07-01">07/01/24 18:27</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I HATE that it's labeled a 'party' fragrance. NO, this is one of the MOST VERSATILE fragrances of all time.<br />
<br />
Sweet, spicy, fresh. It's literally everything you want all year in one bottle. It's also amazing for layering with almost any fragrance. Layer it with a freshy in the summer and man its unique and sexy. This stuff is LIQUID GOLD. <br />
<br />
Don't get me wrong, there are 'better' smelling niche fragrances. But you'll never get such a versatile, beautifully blended, sophisticated scent for this price. Like I can confidently say I often prefer this over a $300, $400 fragrance. Or at least I layer it just so I have some of Ultra Male on me.<br />
<br />
If this ain't the peak of fragrance, idk what is.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="30947"comment_id="2205215"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Jean-Paul-Gaultier/Ultra-Male-30947.html?ccid=2205215#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2203163" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.71);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2133508">rshaunak</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-06-04">06/04/24 04:31</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Ultra male is my most recent fragrance. It is very hyped much like the other JPG fragrances but I think it is the best of the JPG line. At first I get a lavender scent. Then a fruitiness.  I got this for my birthday so I’m unsure of the price but it looks like about £40 for 75ml. It seems like a very good evening fragrance. When you first spray it, it is really sweet but after letting it dry it’s really nice. For me it was sort of a blind buy because I only smelt it on my friend before being bought it but I was not disappointed at all. For any future buyers I think that it is a very likeable scent so a blind buy is okay. It is a very masculine scent as well. <br />
<br />
Silliage is okay. It’s pretty good for a designer.  The longevity is also decent. The bottles design is nice an it’s not tacky at all.<br />
<br />
Silliage - 7/10<br />
Longevity - 8/10<br />
Bottle - 9/10<br />
Popularity - Slightly Overrated</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="30947"comment_id="2177468"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Jean-Paul-Gaultier/Ultra-Male-30947.html?ccid=2177468#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2177377" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.9);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Plus 9pm has better performance. (sorry for comparing but I really do mean all of this)<br />
<br />
Anyways, this fragrance is SUPER sweet throughout all stages of its life. After 20 sec of wearing until the next 6 hours, you get a cloying amount of vanilla, vanilla, and vanilla(a little amber) and that fruitiness that's just floating around the vanilla. There's some bit of freshness from sage, a tiny feel of sharpness from the lavender, but not the scent since the smell is nearly unnoticeable under everything else, and the cedar that's well blended into all of this to make it more masculine and pop out. I love this fragrance but feel like it's a little hard to wear in many occasions. Scent 9.4/10 <br />
<br />
Put 3 sprays on my hoodie and was projecting very well until 4-5 hours in, then it definitely started to tone down more and come in closer than arms length. It did last like that for about another 6 hours though. Longevity 9/10 Projection 8.5/10<br />
<br />
Overall really nice fragrance, but once again, I believe 9pm is better if you're just looking to enjoy the DNA of this or to have a longer performance.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; I decided to buy this fragrance because I once got 4 compliments while wearing the fragrance.I had sampled it from my friend that afternoon.<br />
After three weeks of having it I realised that I was constantly spraying it on myself just so I could smell that opening again and again. I also realised that it’s not for formal wear because it’s a playboy scent probably for younger people around my age. <br />
This doesn’t mean that I don’t like it it’s a fantastic fragrance but in some cases it can be unwearable.<br />
Performance wise it’s very strong on my skin it projects insanely but the longevity doesn’t match the projection so thats kinda disappointing but it is still okay.<br />
You can get it for a fair price these days depending on the website I do suggest that you take the 200ml bottle because you will use it a lot and I mean A WHOLE LOT!<br />
<br />
One of my top 5 favourite fragrances of all time <br />
<br />
Scent:9/10<br />
Projection:10/10<br />
Longevity:7/10<br />
Price:8/10<br />
Overall:9/10<br />
<br />
Hope that you like it as much as I do!!!</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="30947"comment_id="2166721"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Jean-Paul-Gaultier/Ultra-Male-30947.html?ccid=2166721#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2164887" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.83);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:5,&quot;sillage&quot;:4,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2131804">fukofukofuko</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-05-13">05/13/24 14:14</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Hello to everyone! I bought this 125ml version a week ago from the Douglas store in Munich, Germany. The batch of the bottle is dated January 5, 2024. During the opening of the perfume, the sweetness of the pear note hits your face together with the freshness of the mint. This opening is truly remarkable, it is an opening that makes you shine and feel sexy. The perfume loses this freshness on your skin after a while, and is replaced by a more blurry, settled and mature scent that makes me feel calmer, thanks to the cinnamon and caraway. I must say that I am quite pleased with the perfume in terms of scent. The fact that it was said to have a very strong longevity and projection in the old reviews was an important factor in me buying this perfume. The perfume has a very strong projection within 1 hour after you first spray it. However, after the fresh and fruity sweetness that I mentioned for the opening is completely gone, the perfume remains very close to my skin and its projection becomes noticeably weaker. I may be experiencing it this way because the new batches may be weaker in terms of performance or it may be something related to my skin. As a result, I must say that I was satisfied with the scent of the perfume, but I did not get what I expected from the perfume in terms of performance.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; <br />
I have tried several Jean Paul Gaultier fragrances, both feminine and masculine, and I can confidently say that Ultra Male is the pinnacle of their collection (along with La Belle Le Parfum). Francis Kurkdjian did a marvelous job on this fragrance.<br />
<br />
Ultra Male is a sweet masculine fragrance with a delightful blend of pear, vanilla, cinnamon, and lavender notes. Both the opening and the drydown are to die for. The fragrance is very long lasting (10+ hours) and projects quite well. It also leaves wonderful trails behind.<br />
<br />
Overall, a fantastic fragrance! padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2136303" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="dudegetsmoney"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2071768"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.2071768.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="dudegetsmoney" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/Pacific-Chill-81423.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.81423.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Pacific Chill"title="Pacific Chill"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2136303ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck2x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2136303" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.88); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2071768">dudegetsmoney</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-04-25">04/25/24 14:26</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>After buying and wearing most of the popular JPGs, I've come back to Ultra Male to write some updated thoughts.<br />
<br />
It is BY FAR the best smelling, most mass appealing scent by JPG. I hate how people describe it as a solely 'clubbing' fragrance. It's absolutely not just limited to that. t's loud, but not overwhelming at all. It's sweet but not cloying. It's got some spicy freshness to it as well when you first spray it. Drying down to a perfectly toned, delicious cinnamon flavor that has zero woody smells to it. I honestly dislike woody scents, so thank god that Ultra Male doesn't have any traces of woodiness to it, since literally ALL the rest of the JPGs have woody dry-downs. <br />
<br />
An absolute gem. It was the first JPG I bought, so I had high expectations for the rest of the JPGs, but honestly, I was just let down again and again. Or maybe it was because Ultra Male set my standards too high? Either way, perfection in a bottle. It's also 100% wearable in summer by the way, just go light on the sprays, it's doesn't have any of the cloying honey headache smell that Elixir has.<br />
<br />
JPG ratings:<br />
1. Ultra Male<br />
2. Elixir<br />
3. Le Beau EDP<br />
4. Paradise Gardens<br />
5. Le Beau EDT<br />
(I have not tried Le Male Le Parfum yet)</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="30947"comment_id="2136303"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Jean-Paul-Gaultier/Ultra-Male-30947.html?ccid=2136303#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2133680" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.8);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; A loud and sweet scent, great for parties but not limited to such environments, the only time I wouldn't wear this is in summer or more formal occasions. It's got great performance and longevity for me and is maybe more suited to younger crowds. It's a masculine scent but it does feel somewhat feminine due to the sweet pear and vanilla but this is only a slight touch.<br />

Top notes: Pear, lavender<br />
Middle notes: Sage, caraway<br />
Base notes: Vanilla, cedar, amber<br />
<br />
Longevity: 4/5<br />
Sillage: 4/5<br />
Scent: 4/5<br />
Design: 5/5<br />
Gender: Unisex-Male<br />
Overall: 4/5</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="30947"comment_id="2133680"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Jean-Paul-Gaultier/Ultra-Male-30947.html?ccid=2133680#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2133316" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.89);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2114829" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="le male toilet"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2047119"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.2047119.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="le male toilet" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2114829ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck2x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2114829" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.82); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2047119">le male toilet</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-04-05">04/05/24 01:33</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>**Title: The Exemplar of Elegance: A Discursive Analysis of Ultra Male by Jean Paul Gaultier**<br />
<br />
**Introduction**<br />
<br />
Within the domain of fragrances, Ultra Male by Jean Paul Gaultier emerges as a paragon of sophistication and refinement. Crafted under the meticulous purview of Jean Paul Gaultier's esteemed house, this fragrance epitomizes the pinnacle of haute couture olfactory experiences. Esteemed for its impeccable composition and timeless allure, Ultra Male encapsulates a symphony of aromas that evoke a sense of opulence and allure. This treatise endeavors to scrutinize the superlative attributes of Ultra Male, elucidating upon its fragrance notes, enduring longevity, packaging, and overarching appeal.<br />
<br />
**Fragrance Notes: A Rhapsody of Aromatic Complexity**<br />
<br />
At the core of Ultra Male lies a meticulously curated amalgamation of fragrance notes that orchestrates a mesmerizing olfactory odyssey. The top notes inaugurate with a melange of vivacious bergamot and tantalizing pear, instigating a sensory reverie reminiscent of opulent soirées and refined decadence. As the scent unfurls, the middle notes unfurl a tapestry of aromatic splendor, featuring nuances of lavender and mint that imbue the composition with an aura of regal sophistication. Finally, the base notes, comprising vanilla, cinnamon, and amber, culminate in a crescendo of seductive allure, ensconcing the wearer in an ethereal embrace of warmth and sensuality. This meticulously calibrated ensemble of fragrance notes converges to orchestrate a fragrance that is both evocative and enchanting, transcending temporal confines to enrapture the senses for generations to come.<br />
<br />
**Longevity: Endurance Redolent of Elegance**<br />
<br />
An indelible hallmark of exemplary fragrances resides in their enduring longevity, a characteristic in which Ultra Male by Jean Paul Gaultier indisputably excels. Despite the ephemeral nature of top notes, Ultra Male perseveres, unfurling its opulent bouquet with unwavering tenacity throughout the day. Its steadfast presence serves as an emblem of timeless elegance, ensconcing the wearer in an ethereal veil of sophistication that persists from dawn till dusk. Such enduring longevity ensures that Ultra Male remains an indomitable force in the realm of haute couture fragrances, a beacon of refinement and allure amidst a sea of fleeting trends.<br />
<br />
**Packaging: A Reverential Homage to Artistry**<br />
<br />
Beyond its olfactory splendor, Ultra Male captivates the discerning eye with its resplendent packaging that pays homage to the transcendent artistry of Jean Paul Gaultier. Encased within a vessel of svelte contours and opulent hues, the fragrance exudes an aura of regal magnificence, evoking the grandeur of a bygone era. The meticulous attention to detail permeates every facet of the packaging design, from the intricately sculpted bottle to the ornate embellishments adorning its facade. Such exquisite craftsmanship transforms Ultra Male into a veritable objet d'art, revered by connoisseurs and aesthetes alike as a testament to the enduring legacy of Jean Paul Gaultier's unparalleled vision.<br />
<br />
**Overall Appeal: A Fragrance of Universal Allure**<br />
<br />
What distinguishes Ultra Male from its contemporaries is its universal appeal, transcending the constraints of age and gender to resonate with a diverse spectrum of aficionados. Whether donned by the debonair gentleman or the sophisticated femme fatale, Ultra Male exudes an air of unbridled allure that captivates and enchants with equal fervor. Its versatility renders it a veritable chameleon, seamlessly transitioning from daytime rendezvous to nocturnal soirées with effortless grace. In a landscape inundated with ephemeral fads, Ultra Male stands as an indomitable testament to enduring elegance, a perennial favorite among discerning tastemakers and fashion cognoscenti alike.<br />
<br />
**Conclusion**<br />
<br />
In summation, Ultra Male by Jean Paul Gaultier emerges as a magnum opus of olfactory artistry, ensconcing the wearer in an ethereal embrace of sophistication and allure. From its resplendent fragrance notes to its enduring longevity and resplendent packaging, every facet of Ultra Male bears the imprimatur of Jean Paul Gaultier's inimitable vision. As enthusiasts continue to seek out fragrances of unparalleled distinction, Ultra Male remains an enduring icon of elegance and refinement, a timeless testament to the transcendent artistry of Jean Paul Gaultier.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; Young, sexy, masculine with a sensual touch, playful and good performing.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="30947"comment_id="2084907"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Jean-Paul-Gaultier/Ultra-Male-30947.html?ccid=2084907#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div>                            <reviews-infinity :random-colors="[&quot;#fefcee&quot;,&quot;#faf7ec&quot;,&quot;#f9f9f3&quot;,&quot;#f8f9ec&quot;,&quot;#fffdea&quot;,&quot;#faf9fb&quot;,&quot;#faf5f2&quot;,&quot;#f7f4f2&quot;]" :perfume-id="30947" sentiment="all"></reviews-infinity>

Come on!!<br />
Show some respect please!</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="30947"comment_id="591147"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Jean-Paul-Gaultier/Ultra-Male-30947.html?ccid=591147#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent664771" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.84);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc664771" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="PontifexMaximus"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/922344"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.922344.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="PontifexMaximus" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Diesel/Fuel-For-Life-Spirit-17821.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.17821.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Fuel For Life Spirit"title="Fuel For Life Spirit"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma664771ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck6x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd664771" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.84); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/922344">PontifexMaximus</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2016-01-07">01/07/16 13:22</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Jean Paul Gaultier has been experimenting with Le Male flankers for quite some time now, so one shouldn't be surprised to find out the general public was rather skeptical of this release, coming off the heels of Le Male Terrible and Le Beau Male.  Both of those offered something different than the original, sort of, Terrible being a permanent release of a limited summer formula with a little tinkering; and Beau being a rather soft and weak green spring juice with the lavender, wormwood and musk dominating but not impressing the average consumer.  Both were widely panned at the time of their release.  Gaultier's staff finally seem to have been paying attention to the target market of 30 and under consumers with the release of Ultra.  This is 1 Million and L'Homme Intense in its heavy reliance on spicy sweetness and powerful radiance meant for the club circuit.  <br />
The pear in this makes Ultra rather unique, despite sticking to a rather commercial and standard formula.  This pear note is rather shocking in its balance with the rest of the heavier accords, Kurkdijan deserves a good deal of recognition and credit for balancing the whole accord and not taking it in uglier directions after the top notes dissipate like in One Million.  Instead you get a very steady, rather linear club and night scent that knows its bounds but remains a top performer and projection monster without really being a monster at all. The longevity here is outstanding, at 10-12 hours with just 2-3 sprays and sillage is top-flight, but not overbearing like so many other releases born of the same blood.  The sillage on Ultra can best be described as a restrained powerhouse, the balance so brilliantly executed by Kurkdijan that this lacks the imposing qualities of the original vintage Le Male potion.  <br />
The vanilla is still there, the lavender, mint and cinnamon as well, but Ultra takes something very familiar here and injects a major innovation with the pear note, a note that lasts well into the heart of Ultra Male.  A great alternative for those of you looking for something for the winter that could work as a club, date or work scent as long as you are conservative on the trigger.  <br />
<br />
Scent: 4.25 (out of 5)<br />
Longevity: 4.5<br />
Sillage: 5 <br />
Originality: 4.25<br />
<br />
Overall Quality: 4.5<br />
<br />
An outstanding flanker and improvement on previous false starts by the Gaultier house.  Not as original or innovative as Kokoriko, but by playing it safer here and focusing their energies on composition and balance, they've found something original and familiar at once that performs outstandingly, especially in the context of its mid 2010's contemporaries.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1206086">scottgiles86</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2019-12-03">12/03/19 10:41</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I agree with the review below. There is nothing "ultra male" about this scent. Much more feminine than the original. A very strong smell of creamy fruity candy. Vanilla and Pear overload. My wife loves sweet gourmand scents, but this one was much too rich and sweet for her liking.<br />
<br />
Brilliant marketing though. This is definitely a feminine scent sold in a bottle shaped like a male torso to increase sales on both sides. This tactic may fool younger guys, but older men will likely be very put off wearing this. In spite of the numerous youtube and online reviews do not not blind buy this. You must smell it first to understand how strong and obnoxious it can be. It's lasting power is above average and sillage performance is very high...fills up a room with ease. You will definitely get noticed. Do not wear it at work or in formal settings.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="30947"comment_id="1121270"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Jean-Paul-Gaultier/Ultra-Male-30947.html?ccid=1121270#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent647186" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.83);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc647186" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="RedScorpion4"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/21578"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/himg/o.69247.png" class="comments-avatar"alt="RedScorpion4" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Abercrombie-Fitch/Fierce-3508.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.3508.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Fierce"title="Fierce"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma647186ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck4x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd647186" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.83); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/21578">RedScorpion4</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2015-11-11">11/11/15 20:28</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Sampled this while at the mall the other day after the store rep suggested it to me. When I first smelled it, I thought it was way too sweet for my taste, very feminine. I asked two women what they thought of it and they told me that they enjoyed the smell, so I decided to give Ultra a chance to redeem itself. The drydown did not impress me; the amber was very pronounced, cloying almost, and the nauseating sweetness from the opening was still present. If you like sweet gourmand fragrances, definitely give this one a try. Although the smell does not sit well with me, I must admit that Ultra has great longevity and performs like a beast.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="30947"comment_id="647186"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Jean-Paul-Gaultier/Ultra-Male-30947.html?ccid=647186#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent826537" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.9);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:1,&quot;sillage&quot;:1,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%;
